  - ***battle_cinematic_events_tables***:
    - **New fields**:
      - ***key***:
        - **Type**: *StringU8*.
        - **Is Key**: *true*.
      - ***filename***:
        - **Type**: *StringU8*.
        - **Is Key**: *false*.
        - **Description**: *Name of camera.txt file that specifies shots to be used*.
      - ***priority***:
        - **Type**: *Integer*.
        - **Is Key**: *false*.
        - **Description**: *Priority determines if shown as important event and which shots take precedence when selecting shot*.
      - ***level***:
        - **Type**: *StringU8*.
        - **Is Key**: *false*.
      - ***window_in***:
        - **Type**: *Integer*.
        - **Is Key**: *false*.
        - **Description**: *Start of window to trigger, where imagine 0 is when event happens. So if want to start playing/notifying of shot 10 seconds before happens, this should be 10.*.
      - ***window_out***:
        - **Type**: *Integer*.
        - **Is Key**: *false*.
        - **Description**: *End of window to trigger, where imagine 0 is when event happens. So if closest time can play is 5 seconds before, this should be 5.*.
      - ***repeat_wait_ms***:
        - **Type**: *Integer*.
        - **Is Key**: *false*.
        - **Description**: *After a cinematic event is played, it waits this duration until can be played again*.
      - ***event_category***:
        - **Type**: *StringU8*.
        - **Is Key**: *false*.
        - **Is Reference**: *battle_cinematic_event_categories*/*key*.
        - **Description**: *This is the event category, so the type of event the shot gets played for*.
      - ***time_after_event***:
        - **Type**: *Integer*.
        - **Is Key**: *false*.
        - **Description**: *in seconds after trigger event*.
    - **Removed fields**:
      - *New field*.
      - *New field*.

        - **Is Reference**: *character_relationships*/*key*.
      - ***spare_kill_modifier***:
        - **Type**: *Integer*.
        - **Is Key**: *false*.
        - **Description**: *Specifies the modifier that will be used for a character relationship in deciding whether a character will spare/kill in a duel. Use -ve values to add to the "spare" points and +ve values to add to the "kill" points. Range goes from -100 to +100 in code, where -100 is always spare and vice-versa. Note: These modifiers are summed with the ceo_to_duel_outcome_modifiers so if you want to ensure an outcome based on relationship then larger than 100 values can be used to guarantee.*.

Note: These modifiers are summed with the ceo_to_duel_outcome_modifiers so if you want to ensure an outcome based on relationship then larger than 100 values can be used to guarantee.*.
